https://riverdance.com/blog/2012/10/24/jean-butlers-riverdance-dress-contempory-object-of-our-time/	[{"@context": "https://schema.org", "@graph": [{"@type": "WebPage", "@id": "https://riverdance.com/blog/2012/10/24/jean-butlers-riverdance-dress-contempory-object-of-our-time/", "url": "https://riverdance.com/blog/2012/10/24/jean-butlers-riverdance-dress-contempory-object-of-our-time/", "name": "Jean Butler's Riverdance Dress - Contempory Object of Our Time? - Riverdance", "isPartOf": {"@id": "https://riverdance.com/#website"}, "primaryImageOfPage": {"@id": "https://riverdance.com/blog/2012/10/24/jean-butlers-riverdance-dress-contempory-object-of-our-time/#primaryimage"}, "image": {"@id": "https://riverdance.com/blog/2012/10/24/jean-butlers-riverdance-dress-contempory-object-of-our-time/#primaryimage"}, "thumbnailUrl": "", "datePublished": "2012-10-24T15:56:06+00:00", "author": {"@id": "https://riverdance.com/#/schema/person/78374e3b2105783ade33ee0811442e55"}, "description": "It\u2019s made of navy silk velvet, delicate crochet and jet beads, and it was like no other Irish dance dress ever seen before. Jean Butler wore it during the 1994 Eurovision Song Contest interval act she performed with Michael Flatley, and in seven minutes changed the image of Irish dancing forever. Her first dance\u2014soft shoe, delicate\u2014looked traditional, but her sexy, off-the-shoulder dress showed how Irish culture could be reimagined for a modern, global audience. After Michael Flatley\u2019s solo, Butler came back on stage in hard shoes, and their kicks, clicks and taps created a percussive power that resonated further than anyone could have imaged.
